    SELECT "o"."Id", "o"."AutorId", "o"."Cena", "o"."CzyAktywne", "o"."DataPublikacji", "o"."DataWaznosci", "o"."KategoriaId", "o"."LiczbaWyswietlen", "o"."LokalizacjaId", "o"."Opis", "o"."Tytul", "a"."Id" AS "Id0", "a"."AccessFailedCount", "a"."ConcurrencyStamp", "a"."DataRejestracji", "a"."Email", "a"."EmailConfirmed", "a"."Imie", "a"."LockoutEnabled", "a"."LockoutEnd", "a"."Nazwisko", "a"."NormalizedEmail", "a"."NormalizedUserName", "a"."PasswordHash", "a"."PhoneNumber", "a"."PhoneNumberConfirmed", "a"."SecurityStamp", "a"."TwoFactorEnabled", "a"."UserName", "k"."Id" AS "Id1", "k"."Ikona", "k"."Nazwa", "k"."Opis" AS "Opis0", "l"."Id" AS "Id2", "l"."Kod", "l"."Nazwa" AS "Nazwa0", "l"."Wojewodztwo"
    FROM "Ogloszenia" AS "o"
    INNER JOIN "AspNetUsers" AS "a" ON "o"."AutorId" = "a"."Id"
    INNER JOIN "Kategorie" AS "k" ON "o"."KategoriaId" = "k"."Id"
    INNER JOIN "Lokalizacje" AS "l" ON "o"."LokalizacjaId" = "l"."Id"
    WHERE "o"."Id" = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS "t"
LEFT JOIN "Zdjecia" AS "z" ON "t"."Id" = "z"."OgloszenieId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "o0"."Id", "o0"."AutorId", "o0"."DataOdpowiedzi", "o0"."OgloszenieId", "o0"."Tresc", "a0"."Id" AS "Id0", "a0"."AccessFailedCount", "a0"."ConcurrencyStamp", "a0"."DataRejestracji", "a0"."Email", "a0"."EmailConfirmed", "a0"."Imie", "a0"."LockoutEnabled", "a0"."LockoutEnd", "a0"."Nazwisko", "a0"."NormalizedEmail", "a0"."NormalizedUserName", "a0"."PasswordHash", "a0"."PhoneNumber", "a0"."PhoneNumberConfirmed", "a0"."SecurityStamp", "a0"."TwoFactorEnabled", "a0"."UserName"
    FROM "Odpowiedzi" AS "o0"
    INNER JOIN "AspNetUsers" AS "a0" ON "o0"."AutorId" = "a0"."Id"
) AS "t0" ON "t"."Id" = "t0"."OgloszenieId"
ORDER BY "t"."Id", "t"."Id0", "t"."Id1", "t"."Id2", "z"."Id", "t0"."Id"

UPDATE "Ogloszenia" SET "LiczbaWyswietlen" = @p0
WHERE "Id" = @p1
RETURNING 1;
